  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_df2531eb-e5b5-439b-8f64-9ecc5296a8b4'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initializeSiwa();

  <span id="freeText8215365017338546730" style="display:none"><b>They don’t play for the same team. Or do they?</b><br /><br />Jamie Canning has never been able to figure out how he lost his closest friend. Four years ago, his tattooed, wise-cracking, rule-breaking roommate cut him off without an explanation. So what if things got a little weird on the last night of hockey camp the summer they were eighteen? It was just a little drunken foolishness. Nobody died.<br /><br />Ryan Wesley’s biggest regret is coaxing his very straight friend into a bet that pushed the boundaries of their relationship. Now, with their college teams set to face off at the national championship, he’ll finally get a chance to apologize. But all it takes is one look at his longtime crush, and the ache is stronger than ever.<br /><br />Jamie has waited a long time for answers, but walks away with only more questions—can one night of sex ruin a friendship? If not, how about six more weeks of it? When Wesley turns up to coach alongside Jamie for one more hot summer at camp, Jamie has a few things to discover about his old friend... and a big one to learn about himself.<br /><br /><i>Warning: contains sexual situations, skinnydipping, shenanigans in an SUV and proof that coming out to your family on social media is a dicey proposition.</i></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1332168577" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1881759200295279879">Fine, I'll admit it: I was wary going in. <br/><br/>Sometimes when a book is so hyped up, it falls short of expectations. Plus, the authors write mainly M/F, and I did not want a Chicks with Dicks repeat. <br/><br/>Thankfully, what I got was <b>Hockey Players with Dicks</b>. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1438566774ra/15729244.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I approve. <br/><br/><b>Ryan Wesley and Jamie Canning are CRAZY HAWT together, and the sex scenes are through the roof scorching. </b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1431485003ra/14840599.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Jamie figures out he's bi, not just gay for Ryan, which I appreciated (I'm not a fan of GFY, as it mostly strikes me as false).<br/><br/>The alt</span>
  <span id="freeText1881759200295279879" style="display:none">Fine, I'll admit it: I was wary going in. <br><br>Sometimes when a book is so hyped up, it falls short of expectations. Plus, the authors write mainly M/F, and I did not want a Chicks with Dicks repeat. <br><br>Thankfully, what I got was <b>Hockey Players with Dicks</b>. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1438566774ra/15729244.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I approve. <br><br><b>Ryan Wesley and Jamie Canning are CRAZY HAWT together, and the sex scenes are through the roof scorching. </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1431485003ra/14840599.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Jamie figures out he's bi, not just gay for Ryan, which I appreciated (I'm not a fan of GFY, as it mostly strikes me as false).<br><br>The alternative first-person POVs worked fairly well. I did not have trouble figuring out who was talking. <br><br>Some of the dialogue is a little juvenile, as other reviewers have pointed out, but considering that the MCs are 22 and grew up in locker rooms, I found their sometimes crass way of talking believable. <br><br>After all, they are jocks, and this is what (many) jocks are like. <br><br>Plus, when the MCs are alone, their friendship transcends pranks and teasing. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1438566774ra/15729245.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>I loved the synergy between these two! </b><br><br>I know next to nothing about hockey, but the sports talk didn't overwhelm the story. <br><br><b>Honorable mentions go to:</b><br><br>-Coach Pat<br>-Jamie's funfuckingtastic family &amp; their FB responses<br>-Holly for not being a bitch<br>-Condom sofa<br>-Awkward yet steamy sex fest in the backseat of a (rather) small car<br>-Ryan's tattoo (<em>*grabs a tissue*</em>) <br>-Totes feel-good HEA<br><br>Jamie does muse about female anatomy too often at the beginning. I could have done without the many mentions of tits and pussy, fuck you very much. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1438567095ra/15729317.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>But I enjoyed this fairly low angst, sexy as hell, and ultimately sweet estranged-BFFs-to-lovers story. </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1427313228ra/14260924.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer12097475800906421415"><b>Him, HIM, HIIIIMMMMMMMM!!!</b> <br/><br/>Easily one of my favorite books from this year. Easily. And raise your hand if you are surprised?? <br/><br/><i>*crickets*</i><br/><br/><b>This book was aaaammmmmaaaazzziiiinnnggg!</b><br/><br/>I started listening to this book on a road trip with one of my friends, and let me tell you, that car got STEAMY. This book is HOT, and when I got home from the trip, I spent the next five hours listening so I could hear how it ended!<br/><br/>The audio for this book was <b>really, really excellent</b>, and a good audiobook always bumps u</span>
  <span id="freeText12097475800906421415" style="display:none"><b>Him, HIM, HIIIIMMMMMMMM!!!</b> <br /><br />Easily one of my favorite books from this year. Easily. And raise your hand if you are surprised?? <br /><br /><i>*crickets*</i><br /><br /><b>This book was aaaammmmmaaaazzziiiinnnggg!</b><br /><br />I started listening to this book on a road trip with one of my friends, and let me tell you, that car got STEAMY. This book is HOT, and when I got home from the trip, I spent the next five hours listening so I could hear how it ended!<br /><br />The audio for this book was <b>really, really excellent</b>, and a good audiobook always bumps up my rating and improves my feelings about a story. There are two narrators for this story, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/15007880.Teddy_Hamilton" title="Teddy Hamilton" rel="nofollow noopener">Teddy Hamilton</a>, who did the voice of Jamie Canning, and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/3145556.Jacob_Morgan" title="Jacob Morgan" rel="nofollow noopener">Jacob Morgan</a>, who did the voice of Ryan Wesley. I preferred the narration of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/3145556.Jacob_Morgan" title="Jacob Morgan" rel="nofollow noopener">Jacob Morgan</a> for his sexy, understated performance, but both guys did a PHENOMENAL job. There was so much emotion, so much talent in their voices that I KNOW that both of these guys will be on my audiobook radar. Why don't more M/M authors (or M/F, for that matter), use them!? These guys are A-team material!<br /><br />But the story is what got me. Just right in the feels! I just DIED over it. First of all, I'm a huge fan of sexual discovery stories, as I'll call them, and I LOVED discovering Jamie's bisexuality along with him. And loooord, you guys know I love a <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[butt virgin! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. Those sex scenes were SMOKING HOT, with so much sexual tension that I was at the edge of my seat. <br /><br />I'm not usually one to go gaga for sports romance or big, muscle-men, but I think hockey might be the spot where I make my exception. In fact, I've had a great string of sports romances lately, so maybe I should change my tune. <b>Everything in this book, from the hockey details to the kids they coached to the friends-to-lovers story arc, just hit the right note for me.</b><br /><br />This book was veeerrryyy close to making my all-time favorites list, which I'm very exclusive with, and I'm still debating adding this one. It was one of those stories that made me choke up with <b>emotion</b>, and left me feeling raw and happy and overwhelmed. The LOVE is there and so powerful. <br /><br />Awesome job, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/1935000.Elle_Kennedy" title="Elle Kennedy" rel="nofollow noopener">Elle Kennedy</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7737308.Sarina_Bowen" title="Sarina Bowen" rel="nofollow noopener">Sarina Bowen</a>. You both became auto-buy authors for me. <br /> </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1302510635" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9480055724575412047"><b>4 Stars!!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438521955i/15722569.jpg' width='400' height='450' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This was such an adorable feel good story! <i>“Him”</i> was a friends to lovers, GFY story that made me smile or grin more times that I can count. It was sweet, it was sexy, it was simply a fantastic read! Honestly I’m not really a sports romance fan, but I didn’t care about this aspect in this case since this book it’s written by two authors I really enjoy.<br/><br/>Jamie Canning and Ryan Wesley used to be best friends. They used to spend together six weeks every summer at a hockey camp on Lake Placid.</span>
  <span id="freeText9480055724575412047" style="display:none"><b>4 Stars!!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438521955i/15722569.jpg" width="400" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This was such an adorable feel good story! <i>“Him”</i> was a friends to lovers, GFY story that made me smile or grin more times that I can count. It was sweet, it was sexy, it was simply a fantastic read! Honestly I’m not really a sports romance fan, but I didn’t care about this aspect in this case since this book it’s written by two authors I really enjoy.<br><br>Jamie Canning and Ryan Wesley used to be best friends. They used to spend together six weeks every summer at a hockey camp on Lake Placid. Until everything changed between them...Something happened that summer that made Wes to end their friendship, leaving Jamie confused. It’s been nearly four years since Jamie had spoken or seen Wes, but he still misses his friend and occasionally thinks about him. While Wes never returned to the hockey camp, Jamie returned every summer as a coach. <br><br>Wes gets a second chance to make things right with his former best friend when their college teams set to face off at the national championship. From the moment Wes lays his eyes on Jamie, he knows he still has feelings for him. He accepts to coach alongside Jamie on Lake Placid hockey camp hoping Jamie will forgive him and eventually they will be friends again. What he never expected is for Jamie to accepts so easily that he’s gay and also to discover one thing or two about himself. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438521955i/15722570.jpg" width="400" height="512" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>“Him”</i> was a great, sweet and steamy story with two endearing characters that I loved reading about. I liked both Jamie and Wes and I have to say their romance made my heart melt. They were cute together to say the least and I enjoyed seeing them getting to know each other again as friends and later as lovers. I think they complemented each other really well and that’s why their chemistry was so fantastic. It also was done really well and it was palpable from start to finish. <br><br>I enjoyed all kind all m/m romances, but my favorite is GFY m/m novels when one of the characters (or both of them) is (are) struggling to accept the 'new' reality, that he is /they are gay or like in this case bi. While Jamie didn’t struggle too much with everything like I expected, I think his self-discovery felt natural. I really liked how he handled everything he figured out about himself. There’s no stupid, unnecessary drama, (even if the two guys have to face some obstacles) which I enjoyed. <br><br>Like I mentioned above, <i>“Him”</i> was a steamy romance. And when I say steamy I mean steamy-steamy. This aspect of the story was fantastically done. The sexy moments between these two were hot, intense and at times even a little emotional. So to say that I enjoyed them a lot, would be an understatement. Loved every single one of them!<br><br>This novel had also plenty of funny moments. These guys made me laugh as much as they made me swoon. Their banter was so great and I liked how easily they interacted with each other and how every single one of their interactions felt natural. Nothing between them felt forced. Their bond felt real and even if four years had passed since they saw each other, their connection it’s stronger than ever.<br> <br>I have to say one more thing about this awesome read. I loved, loved Jamie’s family. I loved how they were with each other and how wonderful and supportive were not only with Jamie, but with Wes as well.They were pure and simple fantastic!<br><br>All in all, <i>“Him”</i> was a great, sweet and sexy NA m/m romance with likeable main characters, great steam and banter and a tender romance.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438521955i/15722571.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="9480055724575412047" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1303079373" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1303079373" />
    <a title="Geri Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11757728-geri-reads"><img alt="Geri Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1487874758p2/11757728.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1303079373?book_show_action=true">Jun 09, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Geri Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Geri Reads" href="/user/show/11757728-geri-reads">Geri Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1303079373" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer607766634427307780"><b>4.5 stars!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://tinypic.com?ref=t043us' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1438081187ra/15662900.gif' alt='Image and video hosting by TinyPic' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Ryan Wesley and Jamie Canning are best of friends especially during the summer months they spend on Lake Placid where the two of them are enrolled in a summer hockey program. Despite seeing each other for only two months out of the year, they've bonded and considered each other best of friends.<br/><br/>On their last summer there before going off to college, something happened which caused Wes to end their friendship leaving Jamie confused as to why. Fast-forward to four years later and both</span>
  <span id="freeText607766634427307780" style="display:none"><b>4.5 stars!</b><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=t043us" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1438081187ra/15662900.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Ryan Wesley and Jamie Canning are best of friends especially during the summer months they spend on Lake Placid where the two of them are enrolled in a summer hockey program. Despite seeing each other for only two months out of the year, they've bonded and considered each other best of friends.<br><br>On their last summer there before going off to college, something happened which caused Wes to end their friendship leaving Jamie confused as to why. Fast-forward to four years later and both of their teams are in the Frozen Four Hockey tournament.<br><br>By then, Wes is more or less out of the closet and as much as he wants to pursue his feelings for his best friend, he can't because as far as he knows Jamie is straight. An opportunity to coach teen hockey players at the same camp where he and Jamie met gave Wes an opportunity to come out to Jamie do right by their friendship.<br><br>Jamie is still trying to understand what happened all those years ago. And learning about Wes sexuality explained a lot of the decisions Wes made but it doesn't explain Jamie's growing attraction to his best friend. It doesn't explain why he's suddenly discovering stuff about himself, about Wes and about the fact that he wants nothing more than to spend time with Wes and explore the growing feelings between them. And holy sweet mother, did they explore.<br><br>Him is a great gateway M/M read for romance readers looking to try the m/m category. It has great banter, fantastic chemistry and two very likable leads. I admit that Wes annoyed me, at first. He's cocky and he made an arbitrary decision that hurt his best friend. But very early on, he won me over with his sincerity and depth of feelings for Jamie.<br><br>To be honest I was worried with the set-up because Jamie, for all intents and purposes, is straight. But Sarina and Elle did a wonderful job handling that aspect. Jamie self-discovery felt natural. It didn't feel contrived. Both Jamie and Wes have to face obstacles, but when it comes to their feelings for each other, it's clear to me as a reader that they belong together. Their relationship felt raw and sincere, and so, so hot.<br><br>A word of advice. Do not, under any circumstances, read this book in public or even semi-public. I'm not a blushing person but I've lost count how many times, Wes and Jamie made me blush and smile like a lunatic. Both authors captured the emotion perfectly and I just couldn't help but fall in love with Wes and Jamie.<br><br>I really enjoyed this book. And I think that Elle and Sarina's style blended so well it reads like there's only one person writing this book and not two. The writing was seamless and I can't wait to read more from these two, either individually or together.<br><br><i>ARC provided by the authors in exchange for an honest review.</i><br><br>______________________________________________<br><br><b>So this happened. </b><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=23vyzv7" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><b>Of course, I ask myself: Am I going to read it?/</b><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2rgygli" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1433849080ra/15149934.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_1302573549" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1302573549" />
    <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle"><img alt="Jennifer Kyle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514915429p2/9916227.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1302573549?book_show_action=true">Jun 08, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=arcs">arcs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=m-m-f-f-reads">m-m-f-f-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1302573549" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer192600478918984785"><b> 3.75 ~ 4 Stars</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>”They don’t play for the same team. Or do they?”</i>
</b><br/><br/><span>[image error]</span><br/><br/>I’m a huge fan of Elle Kennedy’s <i>Off Campus</i> series as well as Sarina Bowen’s <i>The Ivy Years</i> series and so a collaboration by these two authors made me actually squeal out loud. Now for the iffy area for me is that the genre for this book is mm. The truth is, I have actually only read two others books in this genre. One of them being Sarina Bowen’s <i>The Understatement of the Year</i> which I absolutely loved (felt it clicke</span>
  <span id="freeText192600478918984785" style="display:none"><b> 3.75 ~ 4 Stars</b><br><br><b>
  <i>”They don’t play for the same team. Or do they?”</i>
</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>I’m a huge fan of Elle Kennedy’s <i>Off Campus</i> series as well as Sarina Bowen’s <i>The Ivy Years</i> series and so a collaboration by these two authors made me actually squeal out loud. Now for the iffy area for me is that the genre for this book is mm. The truth is, I have actually only read two others books in this genre. One of them being Sarina Bowen’s <i>The Understatement of the Year</i> which I absolutely loved (felt it clicked all my boxes) however some hardcore mm readers called it mm light. So for me to rate this against others is a bit hard. On the one hand there’s a ton of hot kisses, petting and hot sex scenes. On the other hand, I prefer more drama in my reads but did feel that this one was a good read nonetheless.<br><br>This is a second chance love story so to say, as two best friends make a bet as teens at hockey camp the summer before heading to college. Thereafter, strong feelings of guilt/love on Wesley’s part causes him to cut Jamie’s friendship off without a reason. <br> <br><b>
  <i>”He just cut off contact with me after that summer. He stopped responding to my texts. He just … fired me.”</i>
</b><br><br>The story is told in alternating povs of two hot hockey players. In their senior year of college their respective hockey teams are in the same big tournament and the two come face to face once again.<br><br><b>
  <i>”As I watch Jaime Canning stop another dizzying slap shot. As I admire the grace and deadly precision with which he moves. My weakness is him.”</i>
</b><br><br>Ryan Wesley finds the guts to apologize to his old friend Jamie and he reveals his sexuality and Jamie is ecstatic to have his best friend back. The two start to replay the events that happened between them as teens. Wesley surprises Jamie by showing up at hockey camp to coach and room with him. The attraction magnifies between the two and confuses Jamie. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/492021.gif%20" width="390" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>”I’m attracted to women, no doubt about it. I’m also attracted to men, apparently. Wonderful. Complicated fellow, my dick.”</i>
</b><br><br>The two make a deal that they will end their relationship once they leave camp as Wesley heads for the pros and Jamie waivers on what he wants in his future.<br><br><b>
  <i>”The question now isn’t whether I want to fool around with this man. The question is how I’m ever going to give it up.”</i>
</b><br><br>This story doesn’t have any unnecessary drama and their fall into one another’s arms was well paced and very hot. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1435500672ra/15353772.gif%20" width="390" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Both characters were very likable as were Jamie’s wonderful family. The story has a sweet ending and overall made for a good read. <br><br><b>
  <i>”You really do love me, huh?”<br><br>“Always have.” I swallowed hard. “Always will.” </i>
</b><br><br><i>*ARC generously provided by Sarina Bowen and Elle Kennedy*</i><br> <br></span>

<div id="review_1330588149" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="S.M. West" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/18424676-s-m-west"><img alt="S.M. West" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1564323942p2/18424676.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1330588149?book_show_action=true">Jul 09, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="S.M. West" class="user" itemprop="url" name="S.M. West" href="/user/show/18424676-s-m-west">S.M. West</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18424676-s-m-west?shelf=laugh-out-loud">laugh-out-loud</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18424676-s-m-west?shelf=mm">mm</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18424676-s-m-west?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18424676-s-m-west?shelf=sexy-as-fuck">sexy-as-fuck</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1330588149" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17218389779106377455"><b>4.5 "Purple Skittles" STARS</b><br/><br/>Well this was my first full-on foray into M/M. I’d dabbled before with other stories where it was a side story and had liked it. Now I get the allure…there's something that's almost naughty or sinful about it in a delightfully delicious way! And it's scorching HOT!!<br/><br/><a href='http://imgur.com/RfaKAJD' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437232149ra/15554175.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I’m a big fan of Elle Kennedy, found and fell for her with her Off Campus series, and have never read a Sarina Bowen book before – I’ll be rectifying that STAT. This was a really great, fast, sexy read a</span>
  <span id="freeText17218389779106377455" style="display:none"><b>4.5 "Purple Skittles" STARS</b><br><br>Well this was my first full-on foray into M/M. I’d dabbled before with other stories where it was a side story and had liked it. Now I get the allure…there's something that's almost naughty or sinful about it in a delightfully delicious way! And it's scorching HOT!!<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/RfaKAJD" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437232149ra/15554175.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I’m a big fan of Elle Kennedy, found and fell for her with her Off Campus series, and have never read a Sarina Bowen book before – I’ll be rectifying that STAT. This was a really great, fast, sexy read and the writing style was easy, engaging and seamless; would never have guessed it was co-authored.<br><br>We have two hot college hockey players, Jamie Canning and Ryan Wesley (aka Wes), who were best friends throughout their high school years at Hockey summer camp. But they haven't spoken to each other for four years because of what happened their last night together and now they must face each other. <br><br><a href="http://s1292.photobucket.com/user/swidso/media/HIM_zpslvllps6k.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437526420i/15594837._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo HIM_zpslvllps6k.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Wes has loved Jamie since he was 13 and while he knows they can't have more because Jamie is straight, Wes misses his friend and wants to make amends.<br><br><b>"Canning can't give me what I want, but I still can't stop myself from wanting it. I want whatever I can get - a conversation, a joke gift, a smile, anything. I might not be able to have the steak, but fuck I, I'm fine with some scraps."</b><br><br>The story moves quickly as these two reconnect, work through their past and also come to realize a few things about each other. While there was a lot of sweet and hot sex scenes,...<br><a href="http://imgur.com/rJXv0vH" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437232149ra/15554177.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>there wasn't a lot of angst or drama. There was one little blip but it didn't last for long. I'm not all for dramas sake but would have wanted a bit more of a struggle. <br><br><a href="http://s1292.photobucket.com/user/swidso/media/HIM2_zpsuf6tcaij.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437232149i/15554178.jpg" alt=" photo HIM2_zpsuf6tcaij.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Needless to day, this was a great read and would recommend those who love M/M or either of these authors, or for that matter, if you're feeling adventurous and want to try something new, I say go for it!!<br><br>Now that the cherry's been popped...<br><a href="http://imgur.com/Js4kCNv" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1436734703ra/15497439.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I'll be looking to expand my horizons and am open to suggestions!! <br><br><br><i>***An advance reading copy of Him by Sarina Bowen and Elle Kennedy was generously provided in exchange for an honest review.</i><br><br><b>For more reviews and blog posts.</b><br> <a href="http://slutsistas.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417650623i/12469037._SX540_.png" height="90" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="17218389779106377455" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1302589660" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17365462659545256602"><b>4 Stars</b><br/><br/>When I found out Elle Kennedy was writing an MM... <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1436796169ra/15503837.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>She's about the only MF I read these days! And while I was not as familiar with Sarina Bowen (I did read book 1 of the Ivy League series) I knew her stuff wasn't quite as steamy as Elle's. SO...of course I said a little prayer. Please don't be too YA! <br/><br/>And I was worried for nothing! This one had some really nice steam! I read a lot of MM, so I can't say this one wowed me as far as MMs go. To me it read a lot like Elle Kennedy's Off-Campus </span>
  <span id="freeText17365462659545256602" style="display:none"><b>4 Stars</b><br><br>When I found out Elle Kennedy was writing an MM... <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1436796169ra/15503837.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>She's about the only MF I read these days! And while I was not as familiar with Sarina Bowen (I did read book 1 of the Ivy League series) I knew her stuff wasn't quite as steamy as Elle's. SO...of course I said a little prayer. Please don't be too YA! <br><br>And I was worried for nothing! This one had some really nice steam! I read a lot of MM, so I can't say this one wowed me as far as MMs go. To me it read a lot like Elle Kennedy's Off-Campus series, only with dudes. <br><br>This one was about hockey too. Score!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1436795554i/15503756._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Friends to lovers. I really liked both Jamie and Ryan. Maybe Jamie a bit more. They meet as kids attending an elite summer soccer program. A bet goes wrong and they part ways. They go on to play hockey for different colleges and meet back up at the National Hockey Championships.<br><br>The reason I don't read NA and especially MF is because of the contrived drama. That was my biggest fear with this read. Two people, one who is gay and in love with his former best friend. The other who believes he's straight. Friends with benefits. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1436796169ra/15503838.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>However, thankfully the drama wasn't overdone. It wasn't drawn out. It was resolved quickly. <br><br>There was some good LOL moments. Nothing new and original with the story line but still a very entertaining, enjoyable, sexy read! <br><br><b>
  <i>ARC kindly provided by the authors in exchange for an honest review </i>
</b></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1302371890" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5076135311685163981"><i><b>Him</b> is nominated for Best Romance in the 2015 GoodReads book awards! <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/choiceawards/best-romance-books-2015' rel='nofollow noopener'>Vote here</a>. The only other M/M book nominated is Roan Parrish as best debut author. You can <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/choiceawards/best-debut-goodreads-author-2015' rel='nofollow noopener'>vote of Roan's In the Middle of Somewhere here</a>. <br/><br/>M/M fans <b>REPRESENT</b>!</i><br/><br/><a href='http://gaybook.reviews/2015/07/14/him/him2/' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1446568448i/16832151.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>It is ridiculous, absolutely fucking ridiculous, how much I loved this book. I am a tried and true hockey fan and root for my home team <a href='http://www.google.com/url?sa=t&rct=j&q=&esrc=s&source=web&cd=2&cad=rja&uact=8&ved=0CEoQFjABahUKEwiyxb_a5trGAhUHN4gKHWrODoQ&url=http%3A%2F%2Fwild.nhl.com%2F&ei=pRilVfLeEIfuoATqnLugCA&usg=AFQjCNFn24Mu4E6a88JGEeUzLeWaZZDk3Q&sig2=Kfok3BqJmwfsnm6Mlzda4g' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Minnesota Wild</a> and root for any and all M/M hockey romances. My favorites being <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17410266-frozen-hearts' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>Frozen Hearts</a> by <a href='https://teeganloy.wordpress.com/' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>Teegan Loy</a>, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12989137-home-ice' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>Home Ice</a> by <a href='http://katesherwoodbooks.com/' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>Kate She</a></span>
  <span id="freeText5076135311685163981" style="display:none"><i><b>Him</b> is nominated for Best Romance in the 2015 GoodReads book awards! <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/choiceawards/best-romance-books-2015" rel="nofollow noopener">Vote here</a>. The only other M/M book nominated is Roan Parrish as best debut author. You can <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/choiceawards/best-debut-goodreads-author-2015" rel="nofollow noopener">vote of Roan's In the Middle of Somewhere here</a>. <br><br>M/M fans <b>REPRESENT</b>!</i><br><br><a href="http://gaybook.reviews/2015/07/14/him/him2/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1446568448i/16832151.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>It is ridiculous, absolutely fucking ridiculous, how much I loved this book. I am a tried and true hockey fan and root for my home team <a href="http://www.google.com/url?sa=t&amp;rct=j&amp;q=&amp;esrc=s&amp;source=web&amp;cd=2&amp;cad=rja&amp;uact=8&amp;ved=0CEoQFjABahUKEwiyxb_a5trGAhUHN4gKHWrODoQ&amp;url=http%3A%2F%2Fwild.nhl.com%2F&amp;ei=pRilVfLeEIfuoATqnLugCA&amp;usg=AFQjCNFn24Mu4E6a88JGEeUzLeWaZZDk3Q&amp;sig2=Kfok3BqJmwfsnm6Mlzda4g" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">The Minnesota Wild</a> and root for any and all M/M hockey romances. My favorites being <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17410266-frozen-hearts" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Frozen Hearts</a> by <a href="https://teeganloy.wordpress.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Teegan Loy</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12989137-home-ice" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Home Ice</a> by <a href="http://katesherwoodbooks.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Kate Sherwood</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24656282-winging-it" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Winging It</a> by <a href="http://ashlynkane.blogspot.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Ashlyn Kane</a>.	There is just something about the spike of adrenaline these boys experience on the ice and how they carry that spike over into the bedroom that has my heart leaping and my libido humming. And I can honestly say, even with all the great M/M hockey romances I have read over the years, this one is now my favorite.<br><br>Jamie Canning and Ryan Wesley are two young hockey players on the fact track to the NFL. Both have just graduated from collage and, with their collage hockey careers behind them, Wes will be headed to Canada and Jamie to Detroit in the fall to start in the big leagues. During their summer hiatus, both men work at a hockey camp in Lake Placid teaching the younger generation of greats how to master the game.<br><br>Wes and Jamie met at this same hockey camp when they were in junior high and spent every summer together until they graduated from high school. On their last night of camp, right before both leave for collage, Wes challenges Jamie to a shoot-out, but with some pretty high stakes. Whoever loses has to give the other a blow job. Wes has secretly been pining for his best friend for years and has come to the conclusion that he is gay. Wes thinks that setting up this competition is the perfect solution to get into Jamie's pants and see if the feeling is mutual.<br><br>So, the blow job ends up happening and both men seems to really enjoy it, but Wes has a last minute feeling of shame that he took advantage of Jamie and tucks his tail and runs away, breaking off any and all contact with Jamie for the next 4 years. Jamie is hurt and bewildered but gets on with his life as a heterosexual male.<br><br>Back to the present time, Wes decides he needs to make amends for the uncomfortable, selfish situation he put Jamie in all those years ago and takes a job at the camp as a coach so he can spend one more summer with Jamie. He is still in love with Jamie but he misses his best friend so much that he is willing to put his feelings aside to get that spark back that made their relationship great.<br><br>I don't want to give much more away so you can see for yourselves how these two eventually begin a <b>HOTTER THAN HELL</b> sexual relationship and how they handle their feelings, but I want to tell you to watch for the huge differences between the boy's families and how they grew up. (Remember, they only see each other for 6 weeks a year during the summer from junior high to high school.) It makes all the difference when you reach the epilogue, which is mind-blowingly spectacular and also explains the book's title.<br><br>I absolutely <b>LOVED</b> this book. I sat down to read it and did not move until I was finished. This is a mature, honest look at discovering one's sexuality with a testosterone fueled hockey backdrop and some of the hottest sex I've read this year.<br><br>I can <b>HIGHLY recommended</b> this book to <i>everyone</i>, not just the literary puck bunnies. <a href="https://store.kobobooks.com/en-US/ebook/him-11" rel="nofollow noopener">Him</a> is enjoyable down to the very last line.	Flawless in my opinion. I will be re-reading this when I need a comforting love story that is sure to flood me lots of happy endorphin's.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1433806216ra/15145421.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">	<br><br> This review is also posted at <a href="http://gaybook.reviews/2015/07/14/him/" rel="nofollow noopener">Gay Book Reviews</a><br><br><a href="http://gaybook.reviews/2015/07/14/him/" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1446675884i/16864288.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a>		 </span>
  <a data-text-id="5076135311685163981" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1302624969" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5626757416665945122"><b>5 Stars</b><br/><img src='https://s3.amazonaws.com/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437772551r/15627497.jpg?v=1437772554143' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png' width='50' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>Jamie Canning was my first crush and my first love. But he was never mine to have.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1436909271ra/15517731.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>So let's see here; we have friends-to-lovers, second chance romance and GFY all mixed in with sizzling chemistry and humor. If that's not enough to justify my 5 star rating, I dunno what is. Maybe I haven't read an MM in a while, maybe I was exactly in the mood for a feel good and sexy MM romance? Whatever the reason may be, I loved this book to pieces. There was not one part of it I read where I</span>
  <span id="freeText5626757416665945122" style="display:none"><b>5 Stars</b><br><img src="https://s3.amazonaws.com/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437772551r/15627497.jpg?v=1437772554143" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">Jamie Canning was my first crush and my first love. But he was never mine to have.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1436909271ra/15517731.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>So let's see here; we have friends-to-lovers, second chance romance and GFY all mixed in with sizzling chemistry and humor. If that's not enough to justify my 5 star rating, I dunno what is. Maybe I haven't read an MM in a while, maybe I was exactly in the mood for a feel good and sexy MM romance? Whatever the reason may be, I loved this book to pieces. There was not one part of it I read where I didn't either have a goofy grin on my face or felt like I needed to ice my ovaries. It was fabulous!<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">My weakness is him.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Ryan "Wes" Wesley and Jamie Canning have been friends for years. Some of their favorite memories came from the time they spent together at hockey camp, until the summer when they were eighteen when one night and one dare changed everything and Wes just disappeared from his life. Jamie never stopped missing his best friend or wondering what he did to push him away.<br><br>Wes has been in love with his very straight best friend for years. His mistake those four years ago made him turn away and not look back since. But he's never forgotten Jamie or gotten over his feelings for him. Now chance brings them together again on the ice rink, and Wes will be dammed if he'll just let him walk away from his life again. And if he happens to get his friend to look at him as anything more than just a buddy? Hey, hope springs eternal, right?<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">Maybe one day a switch would suddenly go off and he'd be like, hmmm, I'm totally into Wes. Or maybe he would figure out he swings both ways and decide to take a walk on the dude side.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I simply loved the interaction between Jamie and Wes. Their bond is so strong even after 4 years without speaking. I command the authors for making the transition to Jamie's true sexuality as natural as it did. It was like the reader was discovering everything along with him and it just made it that much better. As for Wes? Don't even get me started on that man. He was my favorite part about this book. He's a rule breaking wise ass, but beneath the muscles and tattoos is a heart of gold. His feelings for Jamie were so heart melting and heart breaking, I just wanted to reach through my kindle and hug him.<br><br>There was so much to love about this book, the biggest being the banter between these two. It was utterly delicious.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">...what two guys stand around describing their perfect sexual partner? Did we wanter onto the set of Sex and the City? If so, I'm Samantha. Called it."<br>"You know actual character names from Sex and the City? Shit, if you hadn't told me you were gay, I would've figured it out just now.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>And if you're curious about the steam? Well let's just say Him has just the right amount to make this story incredibly sexy on top of entertaining as hell! The sexual chemistry between Ryan and Jamie practically crackled with electricity. And when they finally get together? <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437773681ra/15627655.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">We've been going at it every night like puck bunnies in heat this week. Pinch me. It's like a blowjob relay race around here. And we've gotten really good at passing the <i>baton</i></b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422594741ra/13522702.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Ryan was such a fantastic hero as well. He's such a tender heart, but it totally works for him. Together they just made a certain kind of sense. These are two guys that you'll be rooting for from beginning to finish. I absolutely loved the way that Ryan is with his family and their quirkiness. Considering the cold detachment of Wes's family, it was wonderful to have such a warm family dynamic on the other end. <br><br>If you're looking for a fun and sexy NA MM romance, you really should look no further. Sabrina Bowen and Elle Kennedy together are a dynamic powerhouse and I only hope they have more books planned together for the future because I'd read them all without a second thought.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">What do you want?" I ask. And I need him to be specific. This is a very dangerous game we're playing. It will probably end in disaster. But if there's a way I can prevent that, I will.<br>He moves further onto the bed, making room for me. Then he beckons. And there isn't enough money, fame or fortune in the world to keep me from obeying.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437773681ra/15627656.gif" width="200" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437773681ra/15627657.gif" width="200" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>ARC courtesy of authors in exchange for an honest review</i><br><br><b>For more reviews visit<br><a href="http://dirtygirlromance.com" target="blogspot" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1436477285i/15465455._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></span>

<div id="review_1303129748" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1303129748" />
    <a title="Natasha is a Book Junkie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9389992-natasha-is-a-book-junkie"><img alt="Natasha is a Book Junkie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1585046882p2/9389992.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1303129748?book_show_action=true">Jun 09, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Natasha is a Book Junkie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Natasha is a Book Junkie" href="/user/show/9389992-natasha-is-a-book-junkie">Natasha is a Book Junkie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9389992-natasha-is-a-book-junkie?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9389992-natasha-is-a-book-junkie?shelf=standalone">standalone</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9389992-natasha-is-a-book-junkie?shelf=mm">mm</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1303129748" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4214058022908977820"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“Jamie Canning was my first crush and my first love. But he was never mine to have.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/>Be still, my beating heart… It doesn’t happen every day that two authors you <i>love</i> decide to write a book together, so this collaboration had me bouncing off the walls from the moment I got word of it, but this story, this sexy, fun, enchanting story was all I hoped it would be, and so much more. A wonderful testament of both these authors’ extraordinary talents, this is a story that pulled me in from </span>
  <span id="freeText4214058022908977820" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“Jamie Canning was my first crush and my first love. But he was never mine to have.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>Be still, my beating heart… It doesn’t happen every day that two authors you <i>love</i> decide to write a book together, so this collaboration had me bouncing off the walls from the moment I got word of it, but this story, this sexy, fun, enchanting story was all I hoped it would be, and so much more. A wonderful testament of both these authors’ extraordinary talents, this is a story that pulled me in from the very first page, the flawless prose as captivating as the charismatic characters in it, but it was its heart-warming quality and the sheer emotion driving this love story forward, not to mention the blazing chemistry between the two leading men, that owned me cover to cover.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“I have the same damn weakness I’ve always had… My weakness is <b>him</b>.”</i>
</blockquote><br>Former best friends, fellow hockey prodigies, Wes and Jamie used to spend every summer together at hockey camp, until a naughty little bet blurred the lines of their friendship, resulting in four years of silence between them. Now in their early twenties, both of them hockey stars in their own right, they unexpectedly find themselves in the same place at the same time, and memories of some of the happiest moments in their young lives start flooding back, every single one of them tied to those summer camps spent as best friends. But only one of them really knows why their friendship ended so suddenly.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“How do you apologize to someone for cutting them out of your life without so much as an explanation?”</i>
</blockquote><br>As the star player of his college team and with an NHL contract already in the bag, Ryan “Wes” Wesley’s future could not be any brighter, his only regret in life being the loss of his best friend, the only man he’s ever loved, the very reason he was eventually forced to face the truth about his sexuality. His love life now being nothing more than a string of commitment-free hook-ups, Wes enjoys his freedom and ability to focus solely on his hockey career, but seeing his former best friend again stirs up in him feelings he thought were long gone, feelings he’s always known would forever remain unrequited. And memories of a time when those weeks spent together each summer were all he would look forward to all year long.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“My life has been chaotic for as long as I can remember, and I always dealt with it alone. My parents’ criticism, my confusion over my sexuality. But for six weeks every summer, I didn’t have to be alone. I had Jamie, my best friend, my rock.”</i>
</blockquote><br>Jamie Canning never understood why he had lost his best friend from one day to another, always suspecting that their last wager might have affected them differently, but never accepting in his heart that one night of drunken stupidity could have ended a six-year friendship. So when Wes unexpectedly makes contact with him again, Jamie’s heart offers no resistance, eager to have his friend back and desperate for answers.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“Life is just a little brighter, a little louder wherever Wes is.”</i>
</blockquote><br>One last summer before their professional careers take off, one last summer camp as roommates, six weeks to relive old memories and make new ones together—Wes and Jamie might be hoping to rekindle an old friendship, but they end up uncovering much deeper feelings for one another, feelings that would change the course of their futures forever. As they explore each other’s bodies and their own hearts in the process, we watch two young men come to terms with a reality that neither of them ever thought possible, their desire for each other only eclipsed by their unwavering determination to put their friendship first. We watch a young man being finally able to express all he’s ever felt for his best friend after a decade of secretly longing for him, and another young man facing a side of himself he never knew was there, a side that equally confuses and excites him, but also a side of himself he refuses to deny—both their journeys being equally compelling and believable.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“Was I hiding something from myself? Or was there nothing to suppress?”</i>
</blockquote><br>A love story that hooks you in with its simplicity and honesty, I fell in love with every moment of it. It’s a story of two friends becoming lovers, of two men falling for one another and being willing to change their lives in order to put each other first. It is not a story about the struggles of being gay, about coming out to the world or one’s battle with their own sexuality—the focus of the story remains on the irrevocable bond and the sexual attraction between these two men, and the courage it takes to put love first. The perfect blend of sweet and sexy, this tender romance was such a delightful read!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“Loved you every summer since I was thirteen years old. Love you even more now.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><b>[4.5 STARS]</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380382869i/740934.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://www.natashaisabookjunkie.com/2015/07/24/him-by-sarina-bowen-elle-kennedy/" rel="nofollow noopener">See this review on my blog!</a> | <a href="http://www.facebook.com/natashaisabookjunkie" rel="nofollow noopener">Follow me on Facebook!</a> | <a href="http://www.twitter.com/natashabkjunkie" rel="nofollow noopener">Follow me on Twitter!</a><br><br>Amazon US: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/1HuTfLX">http://amzn.to/1HuTfLX</a><br>Amazon UK: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/1Gm8dQy">http://amzn.to/1Gm8dQy</a><br>Amazon CA: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/1HuTk2c">http://amzn.to/1HuTk2c</a></span>

I loved the honesty he had, how he coped with his feelings for Wes. How he let Wes into his heart, STUNNING!<br><br>Wes was also an excellent character, how he loved Jamie but was willing to let him go because he thought he was corrupting him. <br><br>These two were ABSOLUTLELY BEAUTIFUL TOGETHER.       <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1302619798" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3424583974770890484"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1505050565i/23873985._SX540_.jpg' alt='5 stars.jpg (703×245)' width='199' height='69' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I first read this book in 2015...and I was blown away. It was definitely one of the best mm books I read that year, and considering how many times I have re-read this one... it still is.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437244429ra/15557420.gif' alt=' photo giphy 1_zpsvai2zss7.gif' width='289' height='159' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>When I finished it the first time, I wrote a small review for it, but since I have re-read this book multiple times since, ... I figured it deserved more from me. So here goes....<br/><br/>Wes Ryan and Jamie Canning have been best camp buddies for 6 years. Each year, since the age of 12/13 they spend 6 weeks together at "L</span>
  <span id="freeText3424583974770890484" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1505050565i/23873985._SX540_.jpg" alt="5 stars.jpg (703×245)" width="199" height="69" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I first read this book in 2015...and I was blown away. It was definitely one of the best mm books I read that year, and considering how many times I have re-read this one... it still is.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437244429ra/15557420.gif" alt=" photo giphy 1_zpsvai2zss7.gif" width="289" height="159" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When I finished it the first time, I wrote a small review for it, but since I have re-read this book multiple times since, ... I figured it deserved more from me. So here goes....<br><br>Wes Ryan and Jamie Canning have been best camp buddies for 6 years. Each year, since the age of 12/13 they spend 6 weeks together at "Lake Placid" hockey camp, skating their asses off and getting into all sorts of mischief.<br><br>Over the years, Wes' feelings toward Jamie changed though...Instead of just feeling friendly, he started to feel lust and love... On their last day of camp, when they are 18 years old, Wes challenges Jamie to a shoot out. The result of this shoot out leads to the end of their friendship.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1505050565ra/23873986.gif" alt="tumblr_mbui1kpPoU1rxdw8g.gif (500×375)" width="271" height="203" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Fast forward 4 years and these two former best friends are about to cross paths again, when both their teams have to play in the "frozen four". The minute Wes sees Jamie, he knows that his feelings haven't changed. He also realizes that he missed Jamie's friendship, so he decides to offer an olive branch, and try to make things right between them again. Thankfully, Jamie has missed Wes just as well, and he's just as happy to reconnect with his old best friend.<br><br>When Wes decides to join Jaimie at "Lake Placid" once again, this time as coaches, things between them heat up pretty fast.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438160545i/15671282.jpg" alt=" photo Hear-that-sound_zpsemfh5r92.jpg" width="253" height="190" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It doesn't take long for Jamie to come to the conclusion that he is actually bi instead of straight of what's even more surprising is the fact that he's not all that upset about his realization. How could he ever be upset about being attracted to his best friend... who feels the same way about him.<br><br>These boys get pretty hot and heavy... and I loved every single second of it !!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1505050565ra/23873987.gif" alt="879874.gif (500×247)" width="324" height="160" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But summer is about to come to end and decisions have to be made. Jamie has to choose his career path and Wes is ready to go kick ass in Toronto. But what was supposed to be some "hot" fun between them...has changed to so much more. How will they ever be able to be apart again?<br><br>I absolutely loved these two from the moment I started reading. Both characters were awesome, though I have to say that I loved Wes just a tad bit more even though he does make a jerky move towards the end.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1505050565ra/23873988.gif" alt="jaydenkiss GIF" width="283" height="158" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I also loved the fact that Jamie accepted his own sexuality the way he did. There wasn't a lot of drama involved. I think this may also have to do with the loving environment Jamie grew up in. Extra points for Jamie's awesome family !!<br><br>Now, even though Jamie has never been with another man, I would not classify this book as a GFY. Jamie himself states very clearly that it's not just Wes, who can get him turned on. This is more a case of coming to except that you are bi-sexual....and falling in love with your best friend ;)<br><br><b>
  <i>“Loved you every summer since I was thirteen years old. Love you even more now.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438160545i/15671283.jpg" alt=" photo 5292504_zpsmcos46py.jpg" width="272" height="408" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So if you are looking for a sweet, very hot, sports-themed "friends to lovers" story ... you should definitely give this one a go. I highly recommend it ... I would also recommend everyone to read book 2 in this series <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/27797842-us" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">"Us"</a>, which is already published as well  ;)<br><br> <br><br> <br><br> </span>

<div id="review_1342031223" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1342031223" />
    <a title="wesley" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/36179338-wesley"><img alt="wesley" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1446832327p2/36179338.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1342031223?book_show_action=true">Jul 22, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="wesley" class="user" itemprop="url" name="wesley" href="/user/show/36179338-wesley">wesley</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36179338-wesley?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36179338-wesley?shelf=not-your-easy-love">not-your-easy-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36179338-wesley?shelf=sweet-as-sugar">sweet-as-sugar</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36179338-wesley?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36179338-wesley?shelf=friendship">friendship</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36179338-wesley?shelf=second-chances">second-chances</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36179338-wesley?shelf=mm-college">mm-college</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36179338-wesley?shelf=angst">angst</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36179338-wesley?shelf=gay-for-you">gay-for-you</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36179338-wesley?shelf=unrequited-love">unrequited-love</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1342031223" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14083860830027540545"><p>
  <i>This review is long overdue. My life is a giant mess right now. Anyway, here goes...</i>
</p><p><i>Him</i> is one of the few books with a combination of friends-to-lovers, unrequited love, and gay-for-you tropes that I truly and immensely enjoyed.</p><p>During the first chapters, the authors did a marvelous job of piquing my curiosity by slowly putting together the pieces of Wesley and Jamie’s fallout in the past, at the same time building these two characters up which allowed me to establish which side of the person</p></span>
  <span id="freeText14083860830027540545" style="display:none"><p>
  <i>This review is long overdue. My life is a giant mess right now. Anyway, here goes...</i>
</p><p><i>Him</i> is one of the few books with a combination of friends-to-lovers, unrequited love, and gay-for-you tropes that I truly and immensely enjoyed.</p><p>During the first chapters, the authors did a marvelous job of piquing my curiosity by slowly putting together the pieces of Wesley and Jamie’s fallout in the past, at the same time building these two characters up which allowed me to establish which side of the personality spectrum each character belonged to.</p><p>I really thought that Wes is going to be this cocky bastard through and through. Even in Jamie’s POV, there were obvious hints of hero worship for the ever risk-taking Wes. But gosh! Wesley’s internal dilemma was a surefire revelation and totally unexpected.</p><blockquote>
  <b>Canning can't give me what I want, but I still can't stop myself from wanting it. I want whatever I can get --a conversation, a joke gift, a smile, anything. I might not be able to have the steak, but fuck it, I'm fine with some scraps.<br /><br />I just... I just can't let him go yet.</b>
</blockquote><p>I loved how the authors maneuvered Wesley’s secret love for Jamie. It wasn’t exasperating and the way Wesley was allowed to think like an adult – weighing the pros and cons, fighting temptations, doing what’s right instead of just submitting to his lust-filled desires – is commendable.</p><blockquote>
  <b>He's drunk again. Not thinking clearly. For some reason he decided shoving his tongue down my throat was a good idea, but it fuckin ain't. At the end of the day, I'm still gay --and he's still straight. Even worse, I'm still in love with him.</b>
</blockquote><p>Very noteworthy as well is how the authors gave life to the dynamics of Wesley and Jamie’s relationship. Founded on a friendship running deep, both characters have an easy chemistry that readers will surely enjoy uncovering and being a part of. The anecdotes from summers past served to only solidify the relationship arc. The sex was not repetitive and boring. Each time felt like a milestone. It was always comfortable and new.</p><p>For me, this book had everything working together without it trying too damn hard. It had the right mix of humor, tenderness, and sweetness, with some welcomed angst to spice up the storyline, plus strong themes of friendship and family added which tugged at my heart. <b>Five heart-tugging stars</b> for <i>Him</i>!</p> </span>
  <a data-text-id="14083860830027540545" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437564881ra/15598519.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I loved these guys so much!!!Wes is so confident and I like him for this!He is also sweet,cocky,hot and funny!I loved his mouth so much!!Jamie on the other hand is adorable and bossy!Together they are perfection!!When these two are together they are so hot!!Seriously,they are more hot than a F/M couple!It's nice to see 'how these two from best friends become lovers!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437564882i/15598520._SY540_.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If you haven't read before a M/M book you should definitely check this one!!!Two hot hockey players with hilarious and hot moments!!<br><br><br> ARC PROVIDED FOR AN HONEST REVIEW <br><br><br><a href="http://readmore-sleepless.blogspot.gr/" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431941645i/14885109._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </a></span>

<div id="review_1356873139" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1356873139" />

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1356873139?book_show_action=true">Aug 06, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacey is Sassy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacey is Sassy" href="/user/show/12062194-stacey-is-sassy">Stacey is Sassy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/25915423-him">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=kinky">kinky</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=cont-sports">cont-sports</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1356873139" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2811299703248738522"><strong>Acceptance wins the goal...</strong><br/><br/>I started this story with the knowledge that <i>Him</i> was popular, M/M, written by two very talented authors and was supposedly HOT!!! With limited experience reading M/M, I didn't have high expectations and I wasn't sure if it would float my boat. <br/><br/>IT WAS HOT!!!<br/><br/>By the half way point I'm starting to question why this was turning me on so much and analyzing what made it so sexy or sexier than M/f? Maybe it's because women analyze everything and are unsure about getting it rig</span>
  <span id="freeText2811299703248738522" style="display:none"><strong>Acceptance wins the goal...</strong><br /><br />I started this story with the knowledge that <i>Him</i> was popular, M/M, written by two very talented authors and was supposedly HOT!!! With limited experience reading M/M, I didn't have high expectations and I wasn't sure if it would float my boat. <br /><br />IT WAS HOT!!!<br /><br />By the half way point I'm starting to question why this was turning me on so much and analyzing what made it so sexy or sexier than M/f? Maybe it's because women analyze everything and are unsure about getting it right or whether they are on the right track. In a M/M relationship they know what buttons to push because they've got the same buttons. No hit or miss with these guys, no hiding behind fake "o's" is possible. To me it's a confidence thing, two men know what they want and how to get it. Women are still hesitant to ask for what they want and settle for what they get. <br /><br />Wes and Jamie had been friends for years with Wes knowing he was gay and having feelings for Jamie. One decision ... situation ... occurrence that Wes makes, throws their friendship out of whack and leads them to be estranged for four years. They miss each other and when an opportunity presents itself, decide their friendship is worth fighting for. At the time they meet up again, Jamie has a friends with benefits thing going on with a girl named Holly. TBH, this part of the story had me thinking that this relationship would be easier than what I knew would be coming...but you love who you love and sometimes easy is not the best.<br /><br />I don't want to go on too much more but I will say that I loved that there was a storyline outside of their relationship. It kept me interested and I wanted to know more about the intricacies of training and working towards being an elite hockey player.<br /><br />My favourite part of the whole story was towards the end. Acceptance. One word changed everything for me. I read this whole story still with this little voice in my head saying - not too bad for an erotic, take me out of my comfort zone read. Then we get to the part where two blokes have to decide whether to put their lives, careers and acceptance on the line. Is the risks worth it? Will their family's care? Can they live without love? The answers are not the same for everyone. In this story I shed a happy tear and felt content that it all worked out as well as it did.<br /><br />So another comfort zone explosion with no casualties, that left a big old smile plastered on my face. What's next - <i>The life and times of a transsexual vampire yeti</i>? Probably not, but who knows. This year is all about pushing my boundaries.<br /><br />For this review and more visit <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://edgyreviews.com/">http://edgyreviews.com/</a></span>

<div id="review_1303110332" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr"><img alt="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1465384674p2/9080319.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1303110332?book_show_action=true">Jun 09, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
