      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1303110332" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9210631261965573595"><b> 5+ Perfect Friends-to-Lovers MM Stars!<br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Gifs%20from%20AE/771DD62B-4D3B-48DE-AF0E-C7DC83B940CE_zps5ywgckee.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416282263ra/11928344.gif' alt=' photo 771DD62B-4D3B-48DE-AF0E-C7DC83B940CE_zps5ywgckee.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></a><br/><br/><br/>THIS</b> is why I love MM romance! <i><b>HIM</b> </i>has the absolute perfect blend of everything I love about MM romance. <br/><br/>1- Strong, masculine, virile men<br/>2- Friends-to-Lovers trope<br/>3- Gay-for-You trope<br/>4- Endearing secondary characters<br/>5- Humor<br/>6- Angsty tug of war regarding sexual orientation<br/>7- STEAM<br/><br/><br/>Need I say more? In a nutshell, Wes and Jamie have been friends since childhood. Both men are avid hockey players who attended a hockey camp in Lake Placid every summer... until on</span>
  <span id="freeText9210631261965573595" style="display:none"><b> 5+ Perfect Friends-to-Lovers MM Stars!<br><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Gifs%20from%20AE/771DD62B-4D3B-48DE-AF0E-C7DC83B940CE_zps5ywgckee.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416282263ra/11928344.gif" alt=" photo 771DD62B-4D3B-48DE-AF0E-C7DC83B940CE_zps5ywgckee.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br><br>THIS</b> is why I love MM romance! <i><b>HIM</b> </i>has the absolute perfect blend of everything I love about MM romance. <br><br>1- Strong, masculine, virile men<br>2- Friends-to-Lovers trope<br>3- Gay-for-You trope<br>4- Endearing secondary characters<br>5- Humor<br>6- Angsty tug of war regarding sexual orientation<br>7- STEAM<br><br><br>Need I say more? In a nutshell, Wes and Jamie have been friends since childhood. Both men are avid hockey players who attended a hockey camp in Lake Placid every summer... until one stupid bet, a challenge, threw their friendship in the garbage. They hadn't spoken for almost four years until they run into each other in a college tournament, The Frozen Four. Can they get their friendship back? Why did Wes break all contact for all these years?<br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Mobile%20Uploads/2015-08/5A0E97F9-3BA0-4A37-96C7-AEB7A321049B_zpseydnnmxj.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438437468i/15706464._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 5A0E97F9-3BA0-4A37-96C7-AEB7A321049B_zpseydnnmxj.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br><b>HIM</b> is written by the Bowen/Kennedy author duo that I don't believe I've experienced before. Something I'll amend pronto! The writing was flawlessly smooth, with a perfect dose of banter infused to force the reader to smile throughout. The humor brought me back to my personal college days- the pranks between us, the banter between the guys. I'm actually amazed no male author input was in this book as they captured typical male sexual-innuendo verbal sparring in spades!<br><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Next year in Toronto you’ll probably have a personal assistant to carry your stick around for you.”<br><br> It feels superstitious to talk about my NHL contract before the Frozen Four. So I change the subject. “That’s awesome, dude. I love it when another guy holds my stick."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><br>Or better yet-<br><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Like, what two guys stand around describing their perfect sexual partner?” I widen my eyes and look around. “Did we wander onto the set of Sex and the City? If so, I’m Samantha. Called it.”<br><br>The tension diffuses instantly, as Canning’s lips twitch uncontrollably. “You know actual character names from Sex and the City? Shit, if you hadn’t told me you were gay, I would’ve figured it out just now.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><br>A bit of a warning- this book probably shouldn't be consumed in a public venue. People may think you're a bit <i>odd. </i>Smiling, laughing, flushing, fidgeting may ensue. You've been warned. <br><br><br>The <b>angsty build </b> of HIM was perfectly done. One thing about this genre that's an immediate draw for me is that inner struggle within when a man is just coming aware of his attraction to the same sex. Wes had already determined he was gay but Jamie was firmly in denial because he truly loves sex with women too. The authors did a fantastic job with his character- building his gradual acceptance that yes, he's a bisexual man. <br><br><br><b>Secondary characters-</b> coming from a family of six children myself, I loved the cameos from the Canning clan. Thanksgiving was a perfect snapshot of family time within the home of a large, supportive family and it was a great touch. <br><br><br><b>Steam- </b>sweet Jesus. Don't read this amongst anyone who may be able to read <s>your old lady font</s> over your shoulder. It was off the charts hot and I loved the realistic progression of the physical side of their relationship. It was the perfect blend of physical AND emotional for Wes and Jamie. <br><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/M%20and%20M/0D1F3F6D-A4A8-49F5-817F-591DD2CBF056_zpsbng9w8gi.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1438437468ra/15706465.gif" alt=" photo 0D1F3F6D-A4A8-49F5-817F-591DD2CBF056_zpsbng9w8gi.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>I don't even want to count how many times I've typed the word <i>perfect</i> in this review. I could consult a thesaurus but, heck, no other word describes every aspect of <b>HIM. </b><br><br><br>I'd HIGHLY recommend <b>HIM </b>for readers new to the MM genre. The plot-line much like typical Contemporary Friends-to-Lovers tropes but with two hot virile men instead. It's not raunchy. It's a beautiful love story and it reminded me of my first read within the genre. That being said, I have a NEW book recommendation for newbies to the MM genre. <br><br><br>And I thank you, Katy, for this fabulous recommendation. You're a <i>doll.</i><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427478435i/14274945.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i>Advanced copy received by authors in exchange for my HONEST review. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433775460i/15140880.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><a href="http://readescapadereviews.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427480966i/14275361.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> <a href="https://www.facebook.com/readingescapadeblog" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427480966i/14275362.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> <a href="https://twitter.com/readingescapade" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427480966i/14275363.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br></i></span>
  <a data-text-id="9210631261965573595" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

</a><br/> <br/><b>I love M/M it's a favourite Genre of mine. Depending on the read that is and mix that with Friends to lover and Sports Romance... Tick. Tick. Tick we get a really enjoyable read that had me unable to put this book down.</b><br/> <br/>Wes 'Ryan' has been in love with Jamie since he was 13. But after a night of pushing those boundaries and crossing that line Wes felt he pushed Jamie too far and ran for four years. <br/>That is until their paths cross and Jamie decides he's goi</span>

  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437252776i/15558675._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 9140D845-C0F3-4B68-9B1B-1678568DCF3E_zpstpdbprwz.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br><b>I love M/M it's a favourite Genre of mine. Depending on the read that is and mix that with Friends to lover and Sports Romance... Tick. Tick. Tick we get a really enjoyable read that had me unable to put this book down.</b><br> <br>Wes 'Ryan' has been in love with Jamie since he was 13. But after a night of pushing those boundaries and crossing that line Wes felt he pushed Jamie too far and ran for four years. <br>That is until their paths cross and Jamie decides he's going to find out how things pan out and go Lake Placid for 6 weeks of summer camp. He gets 6 weeks to spend time with his old best friend because frankly he misses him, and although Wes may feel guilty Jamie most definitely doesn't want him to feel like that. He wanted that path for himself and not because he was pushed into it. <br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/00DD77C5-C1AA-47B2-AF30-4CAAEB45BE3B_zpslowicgoc.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437252776i/15558676._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 00DD77C5-C1AA-47B2-AF30-4CAAEB45BE3B_zpslowicgoc.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br>They are both drafted to work in the NFL after their 6 weeks which is approaching fast at other sides of the pond. So although this is a romance there is also an amount of where their future is leading <b>Independently</b>. What and where they want to be and yes that includes each other and how they fit into each others lives or not?<br> <br><b>This book is about acceptance and Best Buds falling for their other half...</b><br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/m-m%20kissing/gay%20couple%20cuddling_zpskvjijki8.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437252776ra/15558677.gif" alt=" photo gay couple cuddling_zpskvjijki8.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br><b>It was Sexy, HOT and Intimate......</b><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/m-m%20kissing/gay%20couple%20kissing%20in%20the%20sea_zpsjfexroum.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437252776ra/15558678.gif" alt=" photo gay couple kissing in the sea_zpsjfexroum.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br>Wes is easy going and takes things in his stride yet he also keeps a lot close to his chest because of the family he was brought into. There is a good amount of finding ones self IMO in this <b>GORGEOUS</b> read. I <b>LOVED</b> Ryan he was my kind of guy he really loves easily, yet I suppose he is unable to accept what is in front of him or more like be upfront about his feelings. He though doesn't know how to put himself on the line because he doesn't want to hurt himself nor Jamie. <br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/B66C2018-0A93-4FF2-9609-CCAC98977705_zpsxleyczeb.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437252776i/15558679._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo B66C2018-0A93-4FF2-9609-CCAC98977705_zpsxleyczeb.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Jamie is the <s>straight</s> one yet is he?. Jamie has a very accepting and loving family and that speaks wonders about the kind of person he is and he <b>WANTS</b> Wes and not only for the summer but for the long haul. <br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/BA246475-63B0-4FAE-933C-3796C08131D0_zpsnbmk8qdo.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437252776i/15558680._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo BA246475-63B0-4FAE-933C-3796C08131D0_zpsnbmk8qdo.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>What I loved</b><br>I loved the writing style, I haven't read anything by either of these authors. Yeh I really need to read the DEAL 'especially'. I'm kicking my ASS right now for not doing this sooner, because I sure as hell Loved this gradual journey of acceptance, LOVE, SEXYNESS 'oh my' it had it all Friendship!!! <br> <br>Friends to lovers as I say is a favourite read of mine because there's that connection you feel instantly. You get the FEELS and I most definitely <b>FELT</b> while reading this... <br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/m-m%20kissing/gay%20couple%20holding%20hands_zpswvzld2us.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437252776ra/15558681.gif" alt=" photo gay couple holding hands_zpswvzld2us.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>Top Recommendation from Katy if you love M/M, friends to lovers and sports sexy romances. Then this is your up-next read.</i><br> <br><b>
  <blockquote>Our mouths fit together so perfectly. Every time we kiss, I fall even more in love with him, and it has nothing to do with sex or lust. It's <i>him</i>. His closeness and his scent and the way he soothes me.</blockquote>

They met at a Hockey summer camp on Lake Placid as kids and became the best of friends. As they grew up, the closer they got. When they were both eighteen, they got a little drunk and they made a bet that changed their friendship. Next thing Jamie knows, Wes completely shut him out of his life, and he doesn't know what went wrong. Wes has been in love with his straight best friend for quite a while. That night they shared tortures Wes. He feels responsible for pushing Jamie into doing something he probably didn't want to. He may soon be getting a second chance with his best friend when he finds out his team and Wes's will competing in the same championship. Wes is a star player in his college hockey team and life is pretty good. He has come to terms with his sexuality. He no longer hides it but he doesn't flaunt it either. This was a friends to lovers story which I am totally a sucker for. Not to mention a second chance at romance. I love the connection between them. It left me with a feel good vibe. Overall, it was really great read. It wasn't too angsty or too dramatic, which was nice. It was cute and steamy and definitely something worth reading.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440741644i/16019418._SX540_.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1303270651?book_show_action=true">Jun 09, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="~♡AB♡~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="~♡AB♡~" href="/user/show/12180287-ab">~♡AB♡~</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1303270651" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15876293996583354336">★★★★ <b>4.5 Stars</b> ★★★★<br/><br/><b>Now LIVE!<br/>US - <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://amzn.to/1gYG3GE'>http://amzn.to/1gYG3GE</a> <br/>UK - <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://amzn.to/1esGVBE'>http://amzn.to/1esGVBE</a></b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437469137i/15587697._SY540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>"My weakness is him."</b>
</blockquote><br/>Him, is a second chance romance/best friends to lovers story which I really enjoyed, it was so sweet but had enough going on which kept in me on my toes throughout.<br/><br/>Ryan 'Wes' Wesley and Jamie Canning have been friends since they were 13. Every year for 6 weeks in the summer, they attended a world-class hockey training camp together in Lake Placid, New York and were inseparable. Other than </span>
  <span id="freeText15876293996583354336" style="display:none">★★★★ <b>4.5 Stars</b> ★★★★<br><br><b>Now LIVE!<br>US - <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/1gYG3GE">http://amzn.to/1gYG3GE</a> <br>UK - <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/1esGVBE">http://amzn.to/1esGVBE</a></b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437469137i/15587697._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"My weakness is him."</b>
</blockquote><br>Him, is a second chance romance/best friends to lovers story which I really enjoyed, it was so sweet but had enough going on which kept in me on my toes throughout.<br><br>Ryan 'Wes' Wesley and Jamie Canning have been friends since they were 13. Every year for 6 weeks in the summer, they attended a world-class hockey training camp together in Lake Placid, New York and were inseparable. Other than this, their communication was limited to text messages and the sending back and forth of prank packages.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437472611i/15587901._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When were 18, they made a bet with each other and the consequences of which abruptly end their close friendship.<br><br>Fast forward 4 years and Wes finds himself crossing paths once again with Jamie whilst on the hockey circuit. He has always felt guilty that he cut contact with his best friend and decides to man up and try and make amends. First off, he needs to tell Jamie that he's gay.<br><br>Jamie (who is straight) has always wondered why Wes ended their friendship and although he feels like he should be angry, once he sees Wes again it's as though they had never been apart and after a few awkward moments they soon revert back to their easy and comfortable camaraderie.<br><br>When they come full circle and find themselves as room-mates once again at hockey camp, this time as coaches, it's not long before we are treated to some extremely steamy and emotional moments.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>I'll give him every fucking part of myself, serve it to him like a feast at a banquet. Jamie Canning has no idea the kind of power he has over me."</b>
</blockquote><br>_ _ _ _<br><br>I have been in a bit of a m/m slump for a while now, so this was a surprisingly pleasant read for me. It had just enough drama to keep me going and I really loved the way that Jamie's realisation of his bisexuality was handled. He loved Wes, first as a friend and then when he realised that he loved him romantically, he stood up to the plate and did what he felt was right.<br><br>Wes on the other hand was insecure, but he wasn't shy in coming forward and he had a lot of love to give.<br><br>Already a current fan of Elle Kennedy, I will definitely be checking out more of Sarina Bowen's works.<br><br><b>This is a Standalone M/M Romance told in alternating POV's.</b><br><br><i>ARC gratefully received from the author in exchange for an honest review</i><br><br><a href="http://ilovebooklove-ab.blogspot.co.uk/" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_1302589242" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1302589242" />
    <a title="Mirjana **DTR - Down to Read**" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read"><img alt="Mirjana **DTR - Down to Read**" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1504717217p2/3068938.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1302589242?book_show_action=true">Jun 08, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mirjana **DTR - Down to Read**" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mirjana **DTR - Down to Read**" href="/user/show/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read">Mirjana **DTR - Down to Read**</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=ofy-pan-bi">ofy-pan-bi</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=i-like-your-tats">i-like-your-tats</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=feeeeels">feeeeels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=5-star">5-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=virgins">virgins</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=mm">mm</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=favorite-couples">favorite-couples</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=paperbacks">paperbacks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=talk-dirty-to-me">talk-dirty-to-me</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1302589242" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15566871052059283429"><br/><b>**7/19/2016 - I've missed Wes and Jamie, so I picked up the audiobook. I like having them in my car ;)<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1451914065ra/17620622.gif' height='209' width='500' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></b><br/><br/> -----------------------------------------------<br/><b>***4.9 Stars***</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>My life has been chaotic for as long as I can remember, and I always dealt with it alone. My parents' criticism, my confusion over my sexuality. But for six weeks every summer, I didn't have to be alone. I had Jamie, my best friend, my rock.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br/><br/>How do I feel about this book?<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380358614ra/709788.gif' height='219' width='350' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Typically, I'm not one to read books as soon as they</span>
  <span id="freeText15566871052059283429" style="display:none"><br><b>**7/19/2016 - I've missed Wes and Jamie, so I picked up the audiobook. I like having them in my car ;)<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1451914065ra/17620622.gif" height="209" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></b><br><br> -----------------------------------------------<br><b>***4.9 Stars***</b><br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>My life has been chaotic for as long as I can remember, and I always dealt with it alone. My parents' criticism, my confusion over my sexuality. But for six weeks every summer, I didn't have to be alone. I had Jamie, my best friend, my rock.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>How do I feel about this book?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380358614ra/709788.gif" height="219" width="350" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Typically, I'm not one to read books as soon as they come out...especially books with a lot of hype around them. However, there are always a few exceptions to this, and this book was one of them. A sports romance that's also a friends to lovers??<br><br><img alt="sold-gif" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1438269020ra/15687757.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405306675ra/10380232.gif" height="245" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book had so many things that I love:<br><br>Two endearing and crush-worthy leading men. Seriously impossible not to fall in love with Wes and Jamie....especially Wes! He was this cocky and confident hockey all star that has a vulnerable side he hid from everyone. He's been in love with Jamie from the moment they meet as kids, with every passing summer only intensifying their connection and bond. With the opportunity to fulfill his deepest fantasy with Jamie, Wes will put his heart on the line for one more summer with him. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>I've always kept my memories of Canning to myself. Because they're mine. For six weeks every summer, he was mine.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>I'll give him every fucking part of myself, serve it to him like a feast at a banquet. Jamie Canning has no idea the kind of power he has over me.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>Jamie was just as likable. He was a laidback California guy through and through. He took life as it came and faced everything with an open minded attitude. His growing attraction to his best friend was no different. He wasn't afraid to explore his bisexuality, to experiment, to open himself up to what he was feeling.<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>It's not an exaggeration to say I've always felt a little more alive when he's around. Life is just a little brighter, a little louder wherever Wes is.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>There's a warm feeling in my belly when I look at him. And it's not just sexual. It's...comfortable. Like we're close even when he's twenty yards ahead. I wear a consciousness of him like a second skin.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>Look at those quotes! Come on, how adorable are they? Seriously??<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437401314ra/15581562.gif" alt="description" height="187" width="333" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But this wasn't some mushy love fest...oh no! You get comedy folks...laugh out loud while strangers laugh at you and wonder what the fuck you're reading comedy. Little things that had me cracking up. <br><br>Allow me to set the scene. When Wes and Jamie were younger, they would send each other little gag gifts and presents during their time apart after camp. Just little things that were meant to be funny or a "hey, saw this and thought of you" that would put a smile on the other's face. Well, Jamie happens to find one of these boxes outside of his hotel room door as he's coming back to his room with a teammate...<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>Beside me, Terry scrunches his face in mock terror and wails out, "WHAT'S IN THE BOX?"<br><br>"Dude, nice Seven reference," I say, genuinely impressed.<br><br>He grins. "You don't know how long I've been waiting for an opportunity to do that. Years."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b> <br><br>That right there....my kind of people! <br><br>The banter in this book is phenomenal. You really got the sense of Wes and Jamie's friendship, their camaraderie, their friendship, their humor...just how at ease they were with each other. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"..what two guys stand around describing their perfect sexual partner?" I widen my eyes and look around. "Did we wander onto the set of Sex and the City? If so, I'm Samantha. Called it."<br><br>"You know actual character names from Sex and the City? Shit, if you hadn't old me you were gay, I would've figured it out just now."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b> <br><br>And then...oh boy, and then we have the steam factor. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1438271158ra/15688048.gif" height="281" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>You just know it's going to be good....the exploration and experimentation...I was downright giddy with excitement waiting for it. It did not disappoint. Every kiss, every touch, every rub, every lick....<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1438271745ra/15688194.gif" height="281" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>And then Wes put together 8 of my favoritest words to deliver my favoritest question...<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"Have you ever been acquainted with your prostate?"</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1438271364ra/15688111.gif" height="360" width="599" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If I could have, I would have proceeded reading in a meat locker....because man, oh man....there was no cooling down in sight! These two were combustible! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1427072936ra/14172879.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>Why hasn't anyone ever told me the prostate was some kind of magical pleasure zone? Are there unicorns and orgasm fairies dancing around in there?</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>Based on extensive conversations with numerous friends...Jamie your assessment would be...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1435172187ra/15312977.gif" height="209" width="350" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Alright, I think I need to stop gushing about this book. <br><br>This is the perfect book if you're looking for a great story with fantastic characters, low angst, all heart and plenty of steam. <br><br>Oh, before I forget, let me add....who would have thought that by the end I would totally love Holly?!?! Wasn't she just the most pleasant surprise?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1436883067ra/15514325.gif" height="375" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ok, now I'm really done. <br><br>Wait, wait...let me just take a moment to acknowledge the importance of family. <br><br>To the Wesleys:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1438273012ra/15688352.gif" height="247" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>To the Cannings:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1391112957ra/8332737.gif" height="214" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1438272918ra/15688326.gif" height="281" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Now I'm really done. I mean it. <br><br>Ok, allow me to explain my 4.9 rating. This is just a little pet peeve of mine, but please don't use teenage slang in your books. It totally dates your book. However, if you're going to use it at least be current for the timeline of your book. No one says "whack" or "buggin" anymore. Please and thank you.<br><br>The end. I'm backing away from the computer now. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1438273491ra/15688381.gif" height="300" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>--------------------------------------------<br><br>Elle Kennedy + that blurb = mega cheesy grin for days!! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1391396061ra/8381452.gif" height="300" width="345" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="15566871052059283429" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1333903559" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16356772799356984853"><br/><b>
  <i>** 5+++ “<u>My weakness is HIM.</u>” STARS **</i>
</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You really do love me, huh?”<br/><br/>“ALWAYS HAVE. ALWAYS WILL.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1391418448ra/8384810.gif' width='400' height='230' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>You guys... <b>THIS BOOK WAS PERFECT!</b> ♥♥♥<br/><br/>I don't give a rats a** that it offered nothing new, or that it was pretty much like an M/M version of <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/1935000.Elle_Kennedy' title='Elle Kennedy' rel='nofollow noopener'>Elle Kennedy</a>'s other hockey romances.<br/><br/>I enjoyed every single line and every damn moment between <b>Wes</b> and <b>Jamie</b>. I appreciate that there was <b>NO UNNECESSARILY DRAGGED OUT DRAMA.</b> I appreciate <b>THE SLOW BUILD-UP FOR ROMANCE.</b> (At least for Jamie...) I appre</span>
  <span id="freeText16356772799356984853" style="display:none"><br><b>
  <i>** 5+++ “<u>My weakness is HIM.</u>” STARS **</i>
</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You really do love me, huh?”<br><br>“ALWAYS HAVE. ALWAYS WILL.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1391418448ra/8384810.gif" width="400" height="230" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>You guys... <b>THIS BOOK WAS PERFECT!</b> ♥♥♥<br><br>I don't give a rats a** that it offered nothing new, or that it was pretty much like an M/M version of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/1935000.Elle_Kennedy" title="Elle Kennedy" rel="nofollow noopener">Elle Kennedy</a>'s other hockey romances.<br><br>I enjoyed every single line and every damn moment between <b>Wes</b> and <b>Jamie</b>. I appreciate that there was <b>NO UNNECESSARILY DRAGGED OUT DRAMA.</b> I appreciate <b>THE SLOW BUILD-UP FOR ROMANCE.</b> (At least for Jamie...) I appreciate <b>THE REALISTIC PORTRAYAL OF SELF-DISCOVERY.</b> <br><br>Oh and I appreciate the scorching hoooooot sex, too. Obviously.<br><br><i>What else could a romance reader want in a book, am I right?</i><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Jamie Canning was my first crush and my first love. But he was never mine to have.”<br>~ WES</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1438367436ra/15699000.gif" width="400" height="230" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Ryan “Wes” Wesley</b> has only one regret in his life and that’s losing his best-friend, and first love, after an impulsive, selfish, crazy night. Challenging his best-friend to a bet with a dirty prize, purposefully losing against him and coaxing him into “collecting” the unorthodox prize had given <b>Wes</b> the best, and worst, night of his life.<br><br>Now after 4 years, <b>Wes</b> has a chance to make it right with his ex-best-friend. But how do you apologize to someone for being a terrible friend? For cutting them out of your life without so much as an explanation? <i>Especially if you’re still MADLY in love with them?</i><br><br><b>Jamie Canning</b> is still mad at <b>Ryan Wesley</b> for suddenly disappearing from his life after THAT night. Can one night of drunken stupidity shouldn’t define a 6-year friendship? Can it erase everything beautiful between two people so abruptly? <b>Jamie</b> isn’t bothered with what happened all those years ago, but he can’t get over the fact that someone so important to him could cut him out so easily.<br><br>Now after 4 years, <b>Jamie</b> is once again caught in the crazy wave that is <b>Wes</b>, but something is different this time: <i><b>Jamie</b> has this incredibly potent urge to kiss his lips and let himself devoured by this beautiful boy.</i><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Want you,” I whisper.<br><br>Lately those two words define me.<br><br>“Have me,” he says.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437950254ra/15649845.gif" width="400" height="230" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>OVERALL:</u>
</b> Read it, b*tchez.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>They don’t play for the same team. Or do they?</i>
  </b>
</blockquote></span>

<div id="review_1335037108" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1335037108" />
    <a title="Rachel Reads Ravenously" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously"><img alt="Rachel Reads Ravenously" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1539149211p2/14514998.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1335037108?book_show_action=true">Jul 14, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rachel Reads Ravenously" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rachel Reads Ravenously" href="/user/show/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously">Rachel Reads Ravenously</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/25915423-him">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=ebooks">ebooks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=new-adult-mania">new-adult-mania</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=i-wouldnt-tell-my-mama-i-read-this">i-wouldnt-tell-my-mama-i-read-this</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=sports-romance">sports-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=angsty-intense">angsty-intense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=guilty-pleasure-read">guilty-pleasure-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=m-m-romance">m-m-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=college-romance">college-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1335037108" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4321164707991373861"><b> 4.5 stars! </b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384418777ra/6872834.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i> ^^^me this entire book </i><br/><br/>It's been awhile since I've read a good M/M romance and boy did this book deliver!<br/><br/>Is this book perfect? <b> No. </b> Do I give a shit? <b> Not at all. </b> <br/><br/><b> Him </b> is the story of Jamie and Wes. The two have been summer camp best friends ever since they were 13. They were inseparable, always playing hockey together and playing pranks. The last summer they have at camp changes everything, and Wes completely cuts off Jamie leaving Jamie hurt and wondering what he had done.<br/><br/>Fast </span>
  <span id="freeText4321164707991373861" style="display:none"><b> 4.5 stars! </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384418777ra/6872834.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i> ^^^me this entire book </i><br><br>It's been awhile since I've read a good M/M romance and boy did this book deliver!<br><br>Is this book perfect? <b> No. </b> Do I give a shit? <b> Not at all. </b> <br><br><b> Him </b> is the story of Jamie and Wes. The two have been summer camp best friends ever since they were 13. They were inseparable, always playing hockey together and playing pranks. The last summer they have at camp changes everything, and Wes completely cuts off Jamie leaving Jamie hurt and wondering what he had done.<br><br>Fast forward four years later and both are on their college hockey teams and competing in the same tournament. For Wes seeing Jamie stirs up old feelings he had for his best friend. Spur of the moment he accepts a job coaching at his old summer camp for 6 weeks, alongside Jamie. The two mend their bridges, but as time goes by Wes knows his feelings for his old friend haven't gone away. But Jamie is straight....or is he?<br><br><a href="http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/pagebreak.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421135336i/13327545.png" alt=" photo pagebreak.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This was the ultimate guilty pleasure read. I love GFY romances and unrequited love stories so this fit my tastes perfectly. I loved both of these guys. Cocky, arrogant and yet vulnerable Wes. California golden boy Jamie. Both were suited perfectly to each other and made the best couple. <br><br>An emotional rollercoaster I didn't want to get off of, I read this straight through in a day. Although I ignored a friends advice to not read this in public and ended up blushing and having to put the kindle away until I got home because there are some steamy scenes in this book y'all. So prepare yourselves!<br><br>Recommended for fans of the Try series by Ella Frank, M/M romance readers, and Elle Kennedy fans. Also I've never read anything by Sarina Bowen until this book and I will have to remedy that VERY soon.</span>
  <a data-text-id="4321164707991373861" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('hwdoy6pbSqnCRefx/Aj3xp8oaKchywDjSCWKRTzwjrTkqI8cvqvhImeF0f0XThRv1shpHtBe7JuPmpDKWpT+EQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Fc1SpK8OMr8emfR/I/TSc+tbxnmiAkBC2aB18cxACWN2YrVzu/6ZNLtZwnPIsjHaorvHwFOXrDoeH29+qiR5xg==')})
  }
